They arrested the fugitive Gao Da near the Tingzi Bridge outside the East Gate and took him into temporary custody. Yesterday, Captain Qian prepared a document and sent him to the headquarters for interrogation. It is reported that Gong Guoliang, the chief of the third district stationed in Suzhou, also learned that the robber Gao Da had been arrested in Wuxi and immediately prepared an official document and sent someone to Wuxi to bring him back for legal proceedings. Major Wang approved the request to bring him back for handling according to the law.

Newspaper Delivery Industry Unable to Form Association: Various industries in the county are actively forming industry associations. Previously, ten companies, including the Paibao Office and the Xishan Paibao Society, initiated the formation of an industry association and submitted a request to the County Party Rectification Committee for a permit and guidance. After receiving the report, the committee, due to doubts about the nature of the industry, immediately sent a telegram to the Provincial Party Rectification Committee for verification. Yesterday, they received instructions stating that the nature of newspaper delivery is similar to sales and agency and is not an industrial or commercial activity and thus cannot form an industrial or commercial association. However, since newspapers have been recognized as having a commercial nature and can form associations and join chambers of commerce, it seems appropriate to provide relief to the newspaper delivery industry.

Tragic News of a Girl Crushed to Death by a Car: The Tonghui Road Guangxing Automobile Company in this county is operated by driver Liu Shunrong and is quite prosperous. The other day, one of the company's twenty-fourth car, driven from Meiyuan to the city, crushed to death a girl named Hui Fang (age seven), the daughter of Zhu Zuqi, a resident of Jiangxiang, at Heikou, leaving a bloody mess. The local police officer took the driver Liu Shunrong to the Ninth Public Security Branch, and yesterday, the chief of the Liu Branch sent him to the General Bureau for transfer to the County Court to await interrogation according to law.

Kidnapping Case Verdict in Cheng: Mo, the wife of Fu Sihua Jin Han of Qibei Fang, Qingcheng City, Xiyi, and her daughter, the third young lady, were kidnapped by bandits in November of last year and released from the bandit den the next day, leaving 300 mu of land as collateral for a huge ransom. After reporting the case to the county for investigation, the bandits had already fled far away. The area is located on the border with Jiangyin. In January of this year, Gu Junyi, the head of the Qin Nan Township Security Corps in Jiangyin County, learned that the bandits in the case were hiding in Huangqiao. He immediately went to search, arrest, and detain Zhu Ayuan and Zhu Ajin, two accomplices, and handed them over to the Jiangyin County Government. After repeated court hearings, the facts were clarified yesterday, and Zhu Ayuan was sentenced to one year of imprisonment and Zhu Ajin to eight months to deter others.

Director of the Customs Investigation Bureau Inspects Wuxi: In order to rectify the customs investigation teams in the Suzhou area, the National Salt Affairs Customs Investigation Office of the Ministry of Finance specially dispatched foreign consultant T.M. Lewiston, committee member Wang Fugeng, and inspection office committee member Tang, together with Chen Dexian, director of the Suzhou Customs Investigation Bureau, customs affairs section chief Li Dixin, and staff member Liu Huasan, to inspect the customs investigation units stationed in Shanghai, Wusong, Suzhou, and other places. Yesterday, Director Chen and a party of eight arrived in Wuxi from Suzhou and went to the West Gate to inspect the Seventh Brigade Headquarters of the Customs Investigation and also to the Public Sports Field to inspect the officers and police of the First and Third Squadrons and the Commercial Patrol Team. Director Chen also gave a speech. In the afternoon, they toured the scenic spots and are scheduled to go to Cheng today to inspect the Ninth Team.

The Seat Donation is Still Charged by Restaurants on Behalf: Previously, the Xiyi cuisine industry did not collect the education surtax for self-organized banquets, which affected business. After deliberation by the entire industry, it was decided that the surcharge would no longer be collected from March 1st, and a request was submitted to the county government to maintain this. The county government, according to the provisions of Article 2 of the Collection Regulations, states that Chinese and Western vegetarian restaurants selling seaweed, hotels and inns hosting banquets, cooking boats hosting banquets, and boat owners hosting banquets must collect donations from customers on behalf of the government. The restaurant industry did not receive approval to submit a request to stop collecting on behalf of the government, which is a violation of the regulations. The County Political Affairs Conference resolved that the restaurant industry should still be responsible for collecting the surcharge on behalf. Yesterday, a public notice was issued stating that restaurants and cooking staff must still collect the banquet surcharge on behalf and must not change their names to self-organized in an attempt to evade the charge.

Changzhou 75

Jiangyin Ferry Robbed, People Injured: The Jiangyin-Changzhou ferry departed from Changzhou on the evening of the 13th and returned to Jiangyin carrying goods and more than 30 passengers. When it arrived at Qingyun Pier, Beitang River, as the crew was pulling and preparing to move forward, more than ten bandits suddenly appeared holding pistols and flashlights. They seized the silk rope, swarmed onto the boat, and robbed the boat owner and passengers of more than one hundred yuan in cash and several pieces of gold jewelry. One of the passengers, Bao Quan, whose cash was robbed, grabbed onto one of the robbers and refused to let go. Another robber fired a shot at the back of his head and abdomen, and he was injured. He was taken to Wujin Hospital for treatment on the 14th. After surgery, he was stitched up, but he was still unconscious and his life was in danger.

New Gate Will Have Telephone Communication: The New Gate Town on the Huning Line is closest to Changcheng. The Bureau of Construction once sent a letter to the Jiangsu Construction Department's Electrical Management Office requesting the installation of a long-distance telephone line from Changzhou to Xin Zha. The request was approved, and Deng Fupei, the director of the management office, specially dispatched engineer Li Yangmeng with all the necessary materials. He has arrived in Changzhou and is currently directing the laying of the lines and the installation of the machines. The communication will be available in about four or five days.

Changshu 76

Baiyaotou Robbed Again: Baiyaotou, outside the South Gate, is a must-pass road for Suzhou-Changzhou ships every day. A Di family, who are farmers there, are not very wealthy, but they were coveted by bandits. At about 2:00 AM on the 13th, three bandit boats suddenly arrived with more than 20 people swarming ashore to rob the Di family. They tied up the housewife and beat her severely, forcing her to hand over her belongings. As a result, they were robbed of more than 200 yuan in cash, five dou of white rice, and several pieces of clothing before returning to the boat and fleeing.

Jiangyin 77

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Zhongzheng Township: The Yang Ganhai family in Shuidonggang, Zhongzheng Township, Third District, is of modest means. The other night, more than ten pirates kidnapped Yang Ganhai and his brother, and there is no news of them.

County Rectification Committee Advocates Transfer of Soil Case Jurisdiction: The County Party Rectification Committee, in response to Huang Bingying's report to the Provincial Government regarding Yang Bingwei's discovery of opium in the Chengqin border area, suddenly had mimeographed leaflets circulating on the market on the 6th of this month, titled "Details of the Division of the Jiangyin Giant Soil Case" and addressed to party and government agencies, newspapers, etc. The committee believes that this case should be transferred to another jurisdiction. Yesterday, they specially submitted a request to the Provincial Rectification Committee to forward it to the Provincial Government for an order to transfer the case to another jurisdiction to avoid suspicion. Moreover, Rectification Committee members Gao Kangfu and Meng Yaping stated that the leaflet mentioned that Gao and Committee Member Meng Yaping each received 400 yuan, etc. It is determined that the person who distributed the leaflet is highly suspected to be Huang Bingying based on the circumstances. A special letter was presented to the Rectification Committee instructing the County Public Security Bureau to arrest Huang Fuju on the 13th. That night, Huang was released on bail and was interrogated by County Magistrate Li on the 14th.

Cheng Han Student Suddenly Disappears: Zhu Zhongmu, fourteen years old, the nephew of Zhu Tingqiu of West Main Street, Cheng Han, secretly took out the soft clothing from his house on the 14th and went out without a trace.

Zhenjiang 78

Various Banks Add Branches in Zhenjiang: Since the construction of Zhongshan Road in Zhenjiang, southern industries have gradually become more prosperous, and the population has increased significantly. Various banks in Shanghai have added branches in the city to improve business and convenience for customers. The Shanghai Bank, China Industrial Bank, and Communications Bank have already started operations, and the Central Bank and Guohua Bank are in preparation. The main businesses of each bank are remittance and savings.

Yangzhou 79

Debt-Ridden Man Jumps into River, Revived: Liu Kuiqing, a painter and calligrapher living on Xianliang Street, due to a family quarrel and debt in the early summer of last year, took a car to Liuwei and jumped into the river. His body has not yet been retrieved. The family assumed he was dead and held a funeral. A few days ago, they suddenly received a letter from Liu stating that after jumping into the river, he drifted to the Jiaoshan Koumen and was rescued by a cruiser. After waking up, he was retained as a secretary. For several months, he has been traveling with the warship to Xiamen and other places and has been treated well, accumulating a small amount of salary. He plans to return home soon. The family believes that the trace is correct and has removed the mourning clothes and destroyed the wooden tablet, waiting quietly for Liu to return and reunite.

Nantong 80

Zhang Jian's Leaking Sealed Houses Investigated: The Ministry of Civil Affairs dispatched Li Jin and Zhang Fengzhou to Nantong to divide the provincial and county boundaries. On the 13th, the two officials Li and Zhang returned to Nantong from Dongtai to investigate Zhang Jian's confiscated illegal assets, which totaled more than sixty rooms that had not been sealed. Because they had not been valued, they could not be divided. On the 14th, they returned to the province to ask for instructions.

Problem of Converting Public Funds: The charitable education funds of Nantong that are stored in pawnshops were previously calculated in cash. Currently, due to the conversion into silver dollars, there has been a dispute. The County Government submitted a request to the Judicial Yuan for interpretation, which ordered that the funds should be converted according to the price of cash and silver dollars at the time of deposit so as to avoid one party suffering the loss. However, the public funds were deposited in pawnshops as far back as the Qianlong era of the Qing Dynasty. At that time, there were only silver taels, so it is still difficult to resolve at this time.

Pinghu 81

Haihui Temple Robbed by Bandits: The Haihui Temple (commonly known as Little Putuo) in Caiqi Port, Zhapu, Pinghu, has a substantial income from the spring incense offerings, which has been coveted by bandits. At dawn on the 12th, more than ten bandits scaled the wall and entered the temple with guns. They drove the monks into one room and searched the place, stealing more than 221 yuan in silver dollars and more than 800 jiao in small silver coins, and destroying the utensils. Afterwards, the abbot Pu Yuan asked for the loss list and reported it to the Zhapu Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Central Committee Member Visits Pinghu to Inspect the Eastern Great Port: Zhang Daofan, a member of the Central Committee of the National Government, arrived in Pinghu from Jiashan on the Ningfeng steamship at 5:00 PM on the 14th. He was accompanied by a secretary and Fang Qingru, a standing committee member of the Provincial Party Department, and fifteen others. On the morning of the 15th, the County Party Department convened a meeting of various agencies and organizations and invited Zhang to give instructions. In the afternoon, he took a boat to Zhapu to inspect the Eastern Great Port and then took a car to Haiyan to inspect Party affairs.

Xiaoshan 82

The Third County Executive and Supervisory Committee Members Selected: The Provincial Executive Committee selected the members of the Third Executive and Supervisory Committees of Xiaoshan County on the 11th. Xu, Meng Jinhua, and Chen Lehuan were selected as executive committee members, with Yu Keqin serving as an alternate. Yu Xie was selected as the third County Supervisory Committee member, with Cai Qingfen as an alternate. The commission order has already been received from the Provincial Executive Committee today (14th).

Statistics on Grain Production in the County: The total grain production in Xiaoshan County was the highest in the 19th year. According to the survey reports from the various rural agricultural associations, the total annual production of early rice was more than 298,500 dan, late rice was more than 874,600 dan, glutinous rice was more than 7,500 dan, wheat was more than 950 dan, barley was more than 200 dan, rapeseed was more than 9,800 dan, broad beans were more than 7,000 dan, other cowpeas, edamame, etc. were more than 1,000 dan, and corn was more than 300 dan.

Bengbu 83

Reorganization of Industrial and Commercial Groups Completed: When the people's groups in Bengbu were previously organized, most of them did not follow the regulations promulgated by the Central Government. In order to thoroughly reorganize the situation, the Anhui Provincial Party Department specially dispatched instructors to Bengbu to guide the reorganization. The Bengbu District Rectification Committee approved the establishment. Recently, various industrial and commercial groups have been reorganized. The industrial and commercial associations that have been established include 40 industries, and the labor unions that have been established include 21 industries. The individual stores are still being guided. The executive committee members of each association have been legally produced, and the general inauguration ceremony was held on the morning of the 11th. More than 500 people, including executive committee members, instructors, and guests, attended. Wang Jingzhou, a member of the District Party Department, presided over the oath.

Correspondence 84

Letter from Lawyer Yu Hualong 85

To the Editor: I am writing on behalf of my client, the China Marine Engineers Association, who, after reading the domestic news column of your newspaper on the 12th of this month, found a special dispatch stating that the Daji wheel steam boiler exploded and sank. The location of the incident was Dasheng Port. The cause of the incident was that the ship carried soldiers engaged in customs investigation and dozens of packages of sulfur. Unexpectedly, the soldiers carelessly dropped cigarette butts into the sulfur, causing a portion to catch fire, but it did not spread to the entire cargo, and there was no explosion of the steam boiler. The association has verified that the ship's hull is currently in Shanghai, and the engine is intact. Therefore, the information in your newspaper does not match the facts. The members of the association serving on the Daji wheel have a great reputation at stake and are asking me to write a letter to correct the information. Therefore, I am writing to you to request that you correct the information based on the facts so that the reputation of all the members of my client will not be harmed. Yours sincerely, Lawyer Yu Hualong, March 15th

Educational News

Top News 86

The Organization of City and County Education Associations Can Be Extended to the End of March: The Ministry of Education has issued a circular to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities stating that the organization and reorganization of education associations in various counties can be extended to the end of March.

Official Letter: According to the Guangdong Provincial Training Department and the Guangdong Provincial Department of Education's telegrams stating that it is difficult to complete the organization and reorganization of education associations in various counties and cities within the deadline, and requesting approval for flexible arrangements. The reorganization and organizational procedures for education associations at all levels should still be carried out in accordance with the Education Association Law and the methods for guiding the reorganization and organization of education associations by the Provincial Party Department, Special Municipal Party Departments, and County and City Party Departments. However, the organizational deadline for education associations under the jurisdiction of County and City Party Departments and Special Municipal Party Departments is extended to March 30th. The reorganization and organization should be completed before this date. In addition to the original telegram, which has already been forwarded for reference and will not be copied again, it is hereby replied to the Provincial Training Department and the Provincial Department of Education, and a circular is issued to the Provincial Party Departments and Special Municipal Party Departments of various provinces for compliance. Therefore, I am writing to you to request that you investigate and notify your subordinates accordingly. Official Seal of the Ministry of Education.

City and District Education Association

Each Should Establish One Standing Secretary 87

The City Education Bureau Transmits Instructions to Comply: There is no explicit provision in the Education Association Law regarding whether city, county, and district education associations should establish standing secretaries to handle daily affairs. The Ministry of Education, in order to facilitate the work of education associations at all levels and to unify the organization of education associations at all levels, has telegraphed education officials in various provinces and cities to instruct city, county, and district education associations to stipulate in their respective education association charters that one standing secretary should be established, who will be elected by the secretaries to avoid disputes and to achieve uniformity. The City Education Bureau has already complied with the order and transmitted instructions to the preparatory committees of the various district education associations in the city to comply accordingly.

England Beats Jewish Team Six to Two 103

In the replay of the Shanghai International Football match between England and the Jewish team, which ended in a 2-2 draw after extra time, the game was replayed yesterday afternoon at the Western Recreation Ground. The crowd was even more enthusiastic. As a result, England won 6-2, securing the right to play against the Chinese team in the final. In the first half, the Jewish team took a 2-1 lead and had high hopes, but unfortunately, in the second half, the English team scored five consecutive goals, turning the tide. The Jewish team's lineup remained largely unchanged, while the English team made significant adjustments. Within three minutes of the start of the game, Jewish player S. Greenberg cleverly passed the ball to Pan Keque, who scored. Shortly after, T. Greenberg scored from an oblique angle, making it 2-0. The English team's momentum was not good, so they quickly launched a counterattack. Gray Tormo and Graham both missed shots, but at this time, the Jewish goalkeeper was already busy dealing with the attacks. Eventually, English player Murphy scored a goal, making the score 2-1 at halftime. In the second half, the English team's offensive was extremely strong. Murphy scored another goal, and their momentum increased. The five forwards surrounded the opponent's goal like rapid-fire cannons. In addition, Jewish players Pan Keque and S. Greenberg were injured one after another and could not respond to the attacks. The English team took the opportunity to advance, with Gray Tormo scoring two goals, and Miller and Graham each scoring one goal. As a result, the English team won 6-2. The starting lineups of the two teams were as follows:

England:

Graham, Stoke, Bart, Jewett, Leca, Naer, Duggara, Gray Tormo, Faping, Keane, Murphy, Miller. Jewish Team: L. Greenberg, Qin Sheng, Bu Likehui Er, Tai Quli, M. Greenberg, Pan Keque, G. Greenberg, B. Greenberg, Bu Like, S. Greenberg. Shanghai Secondary Schools.

Shanghai Secondary School Basketball Championship to Begin 104

From March 20th to April 10th, the Shanghai Secondary School Sports Federation Basketball Committee held a meeting at the Sports Association on March 15th. Committee members present included Jiang Jinping (Chairman), Zhuang Xiyuan, Han Kuiyong, etc. The following resolutions were made:

(1) A total of nine schools have registered to participate, divided into "Shang" Group and "Hai" Group. (2) A draw was held to determine the group assignments as follows: "Shang" Group: Guanghua, Jinan, Chizhi, Shanghai Middle School, Pudong; "Hai" Group: Hujiang, Fushi, Fuzhong, Nanshang. (3) The competition dates are from March 20th to April 2nd, every Monday, Tuesday, Thursday, and Friday from 3:00 PM to 5:00 PM at the China Basketball Hall. (4) The winners of the "Shang" and "Hai" Groups (Teams A, B, C, and D) will compete in the final at the China Basketball Hall at 3:30 PM on April 10th. (5) The system will be a single round-robin, calculated by percentage. (6) Referees will be appointed by the China Referee Association. (7) It is stipulated that the game will be 40 minutes long. A team that is more than 15 minutes late will be considered to have forfeited the game. (8) The winning team will be responsible for reporting the results of each game to Mr. Zhang Huiqing of the Association for publication in various newspapers. (9) The prize will be a trophy awarded by the association to the championship team.

Jiangnan University Basketball Tournament Postponed 105

Due to the issue of female player eligibility, the Jiangnan University Sports Association basketball tournament, originally scheduled to begin this Wednesday (the 18th), has been postponed. Because the issue of female player eligibility needs to be discussed at the Executive Committee meeting on the 22nd, the first game on the 18th has been postponed by one week for both men's and women's groups, according to a notice issued by the Standing Basketball Committee.

The "Times" Cup Volleyball Tournament Began Yesterday 106

The Shanghai "Times" Cup Volleyball Tournament has attracted a total of 30 men's and women's teams, an unprecedented event. Yesterday was the first day of the competition, held at the China Athletic Field. A total of 28 matches were scheduled, but one team did not arrive, so only 27 matches were played, from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM. The players were in excellent spirits, and the referees worked tirelessly. Mr. Jiang Xiangqing and Mr. Li Feiyun were particularly enthusiastic. The audience was very enthusiastic. The future of volleyball in Shanghai is very promising, and it will definitely compete with Hong Kong and Guangzhou for the title of national volleyball champion.

Organizational Outline of the North China Games 110

The Preparatory Committee of the 15th North China Games in Jinan publicly elected Committee Member He Siyuan to draft the organizational outline of the conference. After consulting with various sports experts, the draft has been completed. The content of the organization was briefly reported in a previous letter. Here is news from the Shanghai sports community: The organizational outline of the North China Conference, which was previously drafted, has now undergone slight changes. The original plan was to have one chairman, one chief executive, and two deputy chief executives, with two departments below, and a separate Competition Committee. Now, the chairman, chief executive, etc., remain the same, but there are now three departments: Administrative, Engineering, and Competition. In addition, there is a separate Competition Committee. The Administrative Department is responsible for arrangements, reception, publicity, finance, and other matters. The Engineering Department has two divisions: engineering and design. The Competition Department includes registration, refereeing, and record-keeping for track and field events, baseball, softball, and team ball games. The Competition Committee consists of five to seven members and is responsible for resolving disputes arising during the competition and is the highest judicial body of the conference. The amended organizational outline is currently awaiting review by the Preparatory Committee because Director He (Siyuan) is inspecting party affairs and education in Jiaodong. In addition, the provincial government's standing committee today (the 13th) was unable to discuss the budget proposal for the North China Games venue and conference expenses because only four members of the provincial committee were present, which was less than the legal quorum. The proposal to hold a preliminary competition in the province for the North China Games was also not brought up. In addition, the preliminary competition in the province for the men's senior, intermediate, and women's divisions of this North China Games will be organized in accordance with the North China regulations, without distinguishing between senior and intermediate levels. In addition, Shang Shumei, a sports expert from Beiping, was invited by the provincial preparatory committee to Jinan to discuss conference matters. Because of his duties with the upcoming North China ball games, Mr. Shang is scheduled to return to Beiping tonight by train and is scheduled to return to Jinan on April 1st. It is also reported that the date of the North China Conference is scheduled to be held on May 25th. The preliminary competition in the province will be held before May 25th.

Incoming Correspondence

On the Decline of Chinese Fisheries Schools and the Fishing Industry by Li Zuchao 111

The backwardness of various industries in China is a well-recognized and indisputable fact among Chinese people. Taking the Chinese fishing industry as an example, fisheries schools have been established in coastal provinces, with the government investing huge amounts of money to lay the foundation for cultivating talent for the fishing industry. It would be appropriate for talented people to emerge in great numbers, engage in practical industries with rich experience and learning, and strive to build and actively work to reverse the decadent and lazy customs of decades ago. However, today, things have turned out otherwise. When I was studying in Japan, I heard that the fisheries schools in China were divided into two factions, North and South, with teachers and teachers forming factions and students and students also forming factions. Schools are responsible for enlightening future generations, and academic studies should be practical, with training aimed at being useful. What factions are there to divide? Dividing into North and South is already inappropriate. Within one faction, teachers and students should be harmonious and seamless. However, teachers have their own parties, and students have their own factions, like fire and water that cannot approach each other. Is this not even more harsh? Moreover, since this faction is like this, the other faction should learn from this mistake, correct its faults, and not follow in its footsteps. Unexpectedly, they imitate each other and are exactly the same. Within one school, they harbor resentment and slander each other. In that case, between the North and South factions, among the parties of teachers and students, there are even more factions within factions. The competent administrative authorities, in addition to issuing education funds on time, do not pay much attention to the content of the school. When there is a disturbance at the school, they occasionally send one or two people to investigate. Those who are sent are often not familiar with fisheries schools and do not conduct detailed investigations from all sides, but simply ask the principal and complete their duties. How the school's style should be rectified and how academic affairs should be planned are never questioned. Moreover, the principals of fisheries schools are sometimes not from a fisheries background, so they naturally lack relevant knowledge, experience, and qualifications in fisheries affairs. If the principal lacks fisheries knowledge, what good qualities can the teachers have? It is easy to imagine. If the actual situation of fisheries schools is like this, their achievements are also predictable. Now, if you want to seek talent from schools, talk about fishing profits, and develop industries, how can you achieve it? As far as the fishing industry is concerned, the government does not provide adequate protection for fishing boats, and pirates are rampant, allowing them to harass fishermen. Not only do capitalists not dare to risk investing large sums of money in large-scale fishing operations, but even fishermen who have been in the sea for a long time are afraid of it. If this is the case, how can we expect the fishing industry to develop? This is like heading south while wanting to go north. Japanese fishing boats take advantage of the opportunity to enter our territorial waters, and their fishing vessels, seine nets, and hand-operated net fishing boats run rampant in our country's territorial waters without any scruples, so that the fishing profits along the coast are completely invaded. The fish they catch are sold freely in our country without any restrictions. The amount of loss each year is more than hundreds of thousands. This is truly cause for crying and long sighs. The situation of fisheries schools is like this, and the loss of fishing rights is also like that. How can the fishing industry prosper, and how can economic rights not flow out? For the sake of the present, we can only hope that the government will find ways to rectify the fisheries schools. Teachers and students must be made to resolve prejudices, eliminate various factions, and have a consistent spirit. Do not allow teachers and students to use the school to stir up trouble and shout slogans of overthrowing and supporting each other. Teachers should fulfill their teaching responsibilities, and students should fulfill their learning benefits. Talent can naturally rise, and the country will not be so degenerate. As for coastal fisheries, piracy must be effectively prevented, and fishing boats must be protected with all efforts, so that the people of the country know that fishing has great profits and fishing vessels increase daily. If we can develop one part of the fishing industry, we can reduce one part of the invasion, which is much more effective than relying on empty words for diplomatic protests. I humbly offer my views and hope to discuss them with those who pay attention to the fisheries school industry.

Local News

Cotton Production Conference 112

Yesterday, the opening ceremony was held, and two groups of proposal review committee members were appointed. They will continue the meeting at 8:00 AM today. The National Cotton Production Improvement and Statistics Conference held its opening ceremony yesterday at 2:00 PM at the Chinese Merchants Cotton Exchange at No. 80 Avenue Edward VII. The event was extremely grand. Details are recorded as follows:

Attendees: Representatives from the Ministry of Industry, including Mu Ouchu; Zhang Zongcheng and Chen Bingquan from the Ministry of Industry and the Central Promotion Committee; Pan Gongzhan from the Municipal Party Department and Social Affairs Bureau; Feng Liutang and Zheng Hongnian representing the Municipal Government; Zhang Xiangshi representing the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Qi Haishan from the China Cotton Industry Federation; Zou Bingwen, Ye Yuanding, and Cheng Youfu from the Commodity Inspection Bureau; Huang Dingxun from the Industry and Commerce Delegation; Zhu Xianfang from the China Textile Institute; Zhao Lianfang from Central University's Agricultural College; Chen Yanshan from Jinling University's Agricultural College; Li Lubin from Nantong Agricultural College; Wang Jinwu from Zhejiang University's Agricultural College; Rong Zongjing, Guo Le, Guo Shun, Ding Ruoting, Yan Yutang, Chen Zixin, Zhang Zemin representing yarn factories; and over a hundred representatives from provincial cotton fields, agricultural and cotton industry organizations, agricultural and mining departments, and construction departments. Rong Zongjing was elected as chairman, and Ji Zifeng and Qin Xinnong as recorders.

Opening Ceremony Procedures: (1) Bowing deeply to the national flag and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen; (2) Reading the will of Dr. Sun Yat-sen; (3) Silent tribute; (4) Chairman's address (Rong Zongjing); (5) Report by the Preparatory Committee on the preparations; (6) Instructions from the Minister of Industry (represented by Mu Xiangyue); (7) Address by the representative of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department (Pan Gongzhan); (8) Address by the representative of the Shanghai Municipal Government (Feng Liutang); (9) Addresses by guests; (10) Adoption of the conference agenda; (11) Election of the conference presidium; (12) Election of the proposal review committee; (13) Photograph session and adjournment.

Chairman's Address: The long-awaited National Cotton Production Improvement and Statistics Conference has officially opened here today. I am greatly honored that central and local officials have come to give instructions, and representatives from various organizations and groups concerned with cotton planting have come to participate. On behalf of the various organizations that initiated this conference, I extend a warm welcome to all participants. I sincerely hope that under the guidance of officials and with the support of all sectors, China's cotton production will be effectively improved and accurately statistically recorded from now on. This will benefit not only cotton planters and users but also the national economy and people's livelihood. Cotton is the primary material for clothing in our country, and the amount of raw cotton needed each year is enormous. Imports of foreign cotton have been increasing year by year. In 1930, imports of foreign cotton increased to over 2.7 million dan, worth over 100 million taels of silver. At the current precious metal era, the value is even more than that. China ranks third among cotton-producing countries, but solely because production is not expanding and quality is not improving, foreign cotton flows in continuously and money flows out. In the future, there will be a trend of cotton products becoming more refined. If the cotton planting industry does not quickly catch up, expand production, and improve quality, the leakage will be even greater in the future, and the national loss will be immeasurable. In recent years, countries such as the United States, France, Italy, the Netherlands, and Japan have all been promoting cotton planting in their colonies to reduce their dependence on foreign countries for raw cotton. China's soil is extremely suitable for cotton planting and is originally a cotton-producing country, yet it still relies on foreign countries for raw cotton. This is not just a matter of monetary loss but also a shame for the entire nation. A few months ago, when the British economic survey team came to Shanghai and met for the first time, they inquired earnestly about China's cotton planting. Their emphasis on China's cotton planting industry is such that our people should pay even more attention to it. Now, the cotton planting circles in various provinces deeply know that the improvement of cotton production and the detailed preparation of statistics cannot be delayed. Therefore, they have jointly initiated this conference. I am confident that all parties will be able to cooperate consistently to ensure that the raw cotton consumed in our country can gradually be self-sufficient and need not be taken from foreign countries. Furthermore, our country will have surplus high-quality cotton to be transported and sold to foreign countries. This will not only plug a huge leak for the country internally but also open up a huge source of profit for the country externally. This is the ultimate goal of this conference. I sincerely hope that central and local officials will provide various forms of support, promotion, and facilitation to achieve this goal.

Report by the Preparatory Committee: Preparatory Committee member Jiang Dixian reported on the preparations as follows: (1) Origin of the conference: Initially, our Yarn Factory Association has been conducting cotton production statistics for twelve years, but progress has been limited. The biggest reason is the lack of funds, but unfamiliarity with the situation in various places is also a reason. That is, the investigators in various provinces also suffer from the inability to clarify the methods. Therefore, it was proposed to invite investigators from various provinces to come to Shanghai to discuss everything, and there was a plan for a cotton production statistics conference. Later, because in recent years, the investigation of cotton production in various provinces was mostly handled by provincial cotton fields, various parties thought of using this opportunity to contact each other and discuss improvement issues. The scope of improvement issues was very large, and at first, we did not dare to join the conference. However, because most provinces expressed their agreement, it was changed to the Cotton Production Improvement and Statistics Conference. Since the conference was changed to include improvement, there were many people who should be added. However, due to the urgency of time, it was not possible to invite everyone. Therefore, the initiators still adhered to the originally planned one provincial cotton field or farm or cotton industry group per province and our Yarn Factory Association. We sincerely hope that all parties will understand. Fortunately, we all have the same goal of developing China's cotton production, and it does not matter whether we initiate it or not. (2) The improvement or statistics of cotton production requires a lot of money. In European and American countries, the state is responsible for handling it. Now, the domestic political situation is indeed moving towards a better state, but there are still many urgent construction projects that cannot be actively developed. The biggest difficulty is, of course, economic problems. With our strength, we are not enough to talk about this at first. Therefore, the purpose of the conference is not to expect too much results. The biggest hope is to connect the agencies in various provinces that are actually engaged in cotton planting, so that they can exchange reports on the national cotton production situation, get to know each other, and jointly discuss the overall improvement and promotion methods of the national cotton production under the current situation. Secondly, it is to gather cotton fields, farms, or cotton industry organizations from various provinces to jointly discuss the national cotton production statistics and estimation plan. Division of labor and cooperation may make some progress. We deeply know that everyone is currently in a difficult situation. A great plan must be expected in the future and cannot be carried out for a while. However, paying attention to gradual progress within the scope of our capabilities may not be in vain and without benefit to the facts. (3) This conference focuses on research. Therefore, in addition to focusing on the discussion of methods, we also pay special attention to lectures. It is hoped that the pioneers in domestic cotton planting research will give technical guidance to the participants, so that they can return to imitate and implement. Thirteen people have been invited to give lectures, and all the topics have been decided by various parties according to their needs. The topics can be roughly divided into four categories: (1) four people belong to the breeding aspect; (2) three people belong to the promotion aspect; (3) three people belong to the statistical estimation aspect; (4) one person belongs to each of the other aspects, such as inspection, fiber engineering, and cotton industry economy. Whether in academics or in experiments, they all have profound research and will definitely give us an increase in knowledge. This is the common feeling of the representatives and participants of this conference from various provinces. The lecture time has been scheduled and copied on another paper and will not be repeated here. It can be said that the goals of all participants are the same, and it is necessary to adopt the meaning of freedom and fully express opinions from all parties. For example, the issue of the qualifications and voting rights of the participants has been inquired about a lot beforehand. The preparatory meeting yesterday also carefully discussed the results. The qualifications of the participants will not be distinguished, and the voting rights will be based on the number of attendees. That is, we hope to accommodate more opinions from all parties. However, one point should be noted, that is, when discussing a proposal and voting on it, the highest principle is whether the content of the proposal can be implemented under the current situation. However, at present, it seems necessary to pay more attention to the implementation aspect. (5) Personal talent is weak and I cannot bear the responsibility of preparation. In fact, it is impossible to shirk. I have tried my best to do things with many shortcomings, and I am very sorry. I hope that the guests and representatives from various provinces will understand. The preparations for the conference are roughly as described above. Today is the opening day, and cotton industry experts from the country are gathered together. I am really happy.

Minister Kong's Instructions: This time, the Yarn Factory Association and the cotton industry organizations in ten provinces and regions of cotton production jointly initiated the China Cotton Production Improvement and Statistics Conference in Shanghai, which is really a very gratifying thing. Xiangxi is fortunate to be the head of the industry and has infinite hope and optimism for this conference. Now that the military affairs are over and the political tutelage has begun, it is appropriate to gather the common strength of the government and the people to work hard on construction. There are thousands of things to be built. On the government's side, it can only plan for the big and the far, and remove obstacles. The progress of all undertakings depends on the people who have been engaged in the undertaking for a long time, and everyone works hard according to their ability. Only in this way can various construction undertakings be hoped to be carried out simultaneously. This conference is completely initiated and organized by the people's organizations to study the improvement and statistics of China's cotton production, to urge the progress of China's cotton production, and to seek the development of China's cotton industry. This is really a gratifying phenomenon. Because cotton production is one of the most important agricultural products in our country, cotton textile is also the most important industry that once occupied the first place in our country, and cotton products are really necessary for the people of the whole country. The possibility of its future development is very large, and its relationship with the national economy is very close and important. For decades, imports of foreign cotton goods have often occupied the first place in imported goods. In recent years, due to the large quantity of various cotton goods imported, the loss of the national economy is more than 300 million yuan per year. Therefore, it is said that if we want to seek the self-reliance of our country's national economy, we must first seek the full self-sufficiency of cotton goods. However, if we want to achieve the goal of self-sufficiency of cotton goods, it is not only an industrial problem but also an agricultural problem. Because the quality and quantity of cotton production in our country cannot meet the needs of the existing cotton textile industry, the average import of foreign cotton has been more than 2 million dan in recent years. If we further promote the cotton textile industry, the shortage of raw cotton will be even greater. Therefore, if we want to achieve the goal of self-sufficiency of cotton goods, improving and promoting cotton production and developing the cotton textile industry are equally important. This conference brings together cotton industry experts from cotton producing provinces and regions to study and discuss the improvement and promotion of cotton production in our country. The impact of this conference can directly promote the improvement of cotton production quality and the increase in quantity, and indirectly help the development of our country's cotton textile industry. The importance of the relationship is like this. This is why Xiangxi has infinite hope and optimism for this conference. Now, all construction cases require the cooperation of the government and the people. In the future, there are places where government subsidies are needed for various progresses related to cotton production. The government should do its best to jointly promote the improvement and promotion of cotton production to achieve the goal of self-sufficiency of cotton goods and to seek self-reliance in our national economy. Now, at the beginning of the conference, I would like to express my hopes to encourage all attendees.

Address by the Municipal Party Department: Pan Gongzhan, representative of the Municipal Party Department, said briefly that the convening of this grand meeting in Shanghai by cotton industry officials from various provinces expresses great hope. We are all familiar with the national cotton industry and national salvation policy. Cotton production used to be more than 10 million dan, but now it has dropped to 7 million dan. The output has decreased and the quality has deteriorated. Although China has good cotton, such as real cotton, due to various reasons such as mixing of agriculture and commerce and transportation, it is not as convenient as using foreign cotton. Now the production of raw cotton is decreasing, the quality is deteriorating, and the yarn factories are gradually increasing. The progress of cotton production and spindles is not proportional. Therefore, the progress of the national textile industry is tantamount to promoting foreign cotton. If we want to save China, we must make the quality and supply of cotton equal. Now we gather cotton industry experts to discuss improvement. The Municipal Party Department hopes that this conference will have excellent and satisfactory results. Minister of Industry said that the government is very hopeful to cooperate with the people, and the future is promising. If cotton production is improved and the quantity is increased, transportation must be convenient, and the tax rate must be suitable for the business situation. Although this is not directly related, in fact, the development of the cotton industry must be noted. If you have any opinions, please discuss them as much as possible so that the government can refer to them and achieve the effect of cooperation between the government and the people. The Municipal Party Department has no other expectations.

Feng Liutang's Address: Feng Liutang, representative of Shanghai Mayor Zhang, said briefly that Mayor Zhang paid great attention to this conference, but he was unable to attend due to busy official duties. He asked me to be the representative. The first issue of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Principle of People's Livelihood is clothing, and there is also a detailed plan in the industrial plan. The purpose is to supply people with cheap cotton goods. Cotton textile is the first, and the raw material of textile is cotton. If cotton goods are cheap, the raw material must first be cheap, and the quality must also be improved. For example, if you want to spin fine yarn, you must use long-staple cotton. The quality of medium cotton cannot be used for fine yarn, and you have to buy foreign cotton. Now that the price of gold is high, it is impossible to get cheap cotton goods. If you don't achieve self-sufficiency in raw materials, it is impossible. Since the Republic of China, China has paid attention to improvement, and there is still this foundation today, so you have to promote the success of the Yarn Factory Association. However, because you cannot cooperate fully, there are more than 2 million dan of foreign cotton imported today. The United States reports cotton production statistics on time every year, while China's cotton production ranks third in the world. There is very little statistics on this, only the Yarn Factory Association has it, but the omissions cannot be denied. The reason for this is that various parties cannot do their best to assist. Now that representatives of cotton fields and cotton industry organizations from thirteen provinces are gathered to discuss, this answer should be able to obtain good results. Shanghai is originally a cotton-producing area, but on the one hand, it is a concentrated market for the cotton industry, and on the other hand, it is a center for the textile industry. Therefore, Shanghai is very eager for this conference and wishes it to be Lancashire in the West and Osaka in the East.

Zou Bingwen's Address: Zou Bingwen, Director of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, first reported on the past work on cotton crops. In the past, people did not understand and the government did not assist, which caused many difficulties. Now the situation is different. If there is a tight plan and method, contributing to the government and the people will work together to actively carry out, the effect should be more significant. There are three suggestions: (1) have the spirit of unity and mutual assistance; (2) the industry must continue to subsidize based on past results; (3) agricultural improvement is a matter for the government, and I hope the government will be responsible for carrying it out.

Zhang Zongcheng's Address: Zhang Zongcheng, representative of the Central Agricultural Promotion Committee, said briefly that the first priority of nation-building is people's livelihood, and people's livelihood is especially important for clothing. The importance of cotton for the needs of the people is evident. This conference opens a new era in the history of China's cotton industry. However, the importance of the conference lies in the results of the conference. This association is a collection of cotton planting organizations and textile industry groups. There are experts and government representatives. The results can be expected to be satisfactory. There have been many grand conferences in the past, but the results are very vague. I hope that experts will contribute all the crystallized research results to the cotton industry organizations, report the achievements they have obtained for research, and discuss how to divide the work, how to cooperate, and jointly seek the progress of China's cotton industry.

Mu Ouchu's Speech: Mu Ouchu, former Vice Minister of Industry and Commerce, said briefly that today we gather national cotton industry experts and representatives of competent authorities from various provinces in one room to study and discuss the improvement and statistics of cotton production in our country. It is really an unprecedented grand event. Xiangyue is very happy to be able to attend this event. The reason why all undertakings in our country are not developed is that agriculture, industry, commerce, and academics cannot be united and connected. Those engaged in agriculture, industry, and commerce often do not know academics, and those engaged in academics often do not know agriculture, industry, and commerce. However, if you want to seek the development of an undertaking, the fundamental basis is in academics. The political evolution and industrial development of European, American, and Japanese countries are completely based on advanced science. Industrial revolution is caused by scientific invention, and industrial revolution affects social organization and political organization. The result is industrial scientization and political scientization. Not only industrial countries are like this, but agricultural countries are also scientifically washed by scientific inventions and industrial revolutions, and the result is agricultural scientization. So, to sum up, the development of all undertakings in European, American, and Japanese countries is based on advanced science, while our country is not. Our country's old culture has always focused on literature and philosophy, and lacks science. Therefore, the general public not only has no scientific inventions, but also lacks scientific literacy. With such a lack of scientific foundation, the people are also in the era of world transportation. European, American, and Japanese countries, with their mass-produced products after scientific inventions and industrial revolutions, came to China like a surging tide, making our country completely unable to resist and had to succumb to this world trend and be forced to trade. Therefore, in the decades of trade between China and foreign countries, China's commerce has shown unprecedented development, but it is completely passive. The agriculture and industry of this country are still in their infancy and have not yet reached the stage of development. The so-called commercial development is not due to the development of agriculture and industry in this country, but is developed from actually speaking, the bulk of commerce is completely burdened with foreign goods to promote sales for foreigners. Therefore, the more developed the commerce, the more difficult the national economy, and the more difficult the national livelihood. The only reason is that the agriculture and industry of our country do not have advanced science as their foundation, and the development of all commerce is passive. The same is true of the cotton industry. Xiangyue has seen this and deeply knows the importance of agronomy and the relationship between cotton production and our country, and has been committed to this for 20 years. It is only that there are few people and it is not easy to see the effect. Fortunately, the general trend is that the people of the country have a deep understanding of this, and everyone knows that the cotton textile industry is the pioneer of developing industry, and the improvement of cotton production is a necessary foundation for promoting the cotton textile industry. At the beginning of the national government's political tutelage, it focuses on construction, encourages progress, and rewards talents. At this time, you gentlemen are holding this unprecedented conference to conduct practical research on the improvement and promotion of cotton production. All the gentlemen attending the meeting are cotton industry experts and have deep research on all aspects of cotton production issues. There is no need for Xiangyue to say more. The results of this conference will definitely have a very good impact on the future of cotton production. Xiangyue is overjoyed and sincerely hopes that you gentlemen will use scientific methods to improve cotton production and economic methods to promote cotton production, so that the future of cotton production in our country will become increasingly developed and can be on par with the cotton production of the United States of America to benefit cotton farmers and the entire national economy. I am willing to pray to the end. Then Vice Minister Zheng of the Ministry of Industry successively gave speeches, the main idea of which was that we should cooperate to seek improvement.

Appointment of Various Officials: (A) The presidium of the conference is: Jiangsu: Lu Feishu; Shanghai Yarn Factory Association: Nie Lusheng; Hubei: Yang Xiandong; Zhejiang: Fang Junqiang; Shandong: Hu Pingchu; Hubei: Yuan Zhongkui; Shaanxi: Li Guozhen. (B) The proposal review committee is: Improvement Group: Sun Enqing, Chen Yanshan, Li Lubin, Fang Junqiang, Yuan Cukui, Hu Pingchu, Zhang Zemin, Zhao Lianfang, Ye Yuanding (9 people); Statistics Group: Jiang Dixian, Du Xingtang, Liu Shenghuang, Wu Weijing, Chen Bingquan, Wang Jinwu, Jiang Hanluo (7 people). (C) Conference Secretaries: Jiang Dixian, Qin Xinnong, Wu Weijing. After the appointment of the various officials, a photograph was taken and the meeting adjourned. In the evening, the Yarn Factory Association hosted a banquet for the attending representatives at the Daguanlou.

Today's Agenda: The meeting will be held at 8:00 AM this morning. After the reports from Liaoning, Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, there will be lectures. The originally scheduled Mr. Feng Qifu has been temporarily changed to Mr. Zhao Lianfang. At 1:30 PM, Lu Feishu will talk about agricultural promotion, Tan Zhongyue will talk about the process of improving Chicken Foot Cotton at Nantong Agricultural University and the future breeding design. Letter from the Money Trade Association to the Chamber of Commerce

Advocating the Final Account Period 115

The end of February is difficult to implement. The end of January is more suitable. The Shanghai Money Trade Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce: In reply, we received a letter stating that the closing date for the 20th year should be planned in advance. We read in the newspaper that the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau submitted a document to the mayor proposing that from the 20th year, the accounting year for national industry and commerce be changed to from March 1 of this year to the end of February of the following year. The first closing and submission period each year is the end of June, the second is the end of October, and the third final closing period is the end of February of the following year. This is really suitable for both government orders and commercial sentiment. It is proposed to separately send telegrams to the municipal government and the Executive Yuan to express approval. Therefore, we sent letters to various industry associations to solicit opinions, asking them to provide detailed opinions on the above-mentioned revised closing date method before March 15, so that we can handle it. The association has submitted it to the members' meeting for detailed discussion. The Qian agreed that the closing of accounts is a matter of transfer and is extremely important. If the closing period is not appropriate, the business will be affected. The total closing period of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau's proposal at the end of February seems to give merchants ample time to prepare, but I don't know that the obstruction is equal to its lack of time. The income and sales of agricultural products are based on solar terms. By January, they can all be completely stored. Farmers use the proceeds as compensation for the goods in the store. All over the country, it has become a rule. If the closing of accounts is delayed until the end of February, the proceeds will often be used for other consumption after a long period of time. Then the store's collection of accounts will inevitably be difficult. The inappropriate one is that from the end of February, farmers will engage in spring farming, and merchants will be in the peak period of entering spring goods. It is the time for financial adjustment, but it is the period for collection and termination. The inappropriate one is that the Qian industry is customary to start business after the total relief and after going through sorting and investigation procedures. The shortest time for sorting and investigation also takes half a month. If the total closing period is the end of February, then the Qian industry will grant relief after mid-March, which will inevitably affect the progress of various industries. The inappropriate one is three. In summary, the Qian agreed that the total closing period at the end of February is difficult to implement. After repeated consideration, it is proposed that the total closing period at the end of January is more suitable. At this time, both agricultural products and commercial goods can be terminated. There is no inconvenience as mentioned above, and it also implicitly conforms to the proposal to have the day before the beginning of spring as the total closing and submission date. The whole body unanimously agreed that it is the most suitable and feasible. The case is especially the opinion of the association is hereby conveyed in a letter. Please carefully consider the business situation and adopt it. I am extremely grateful. This reply is to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce.

A major reform

Vehicle Timetable on Both Lines 116

Using new locomotives, shorten travel time, change stops for the convenience of passengers between Beijing and Shanghai.

(A) Special Express Trains

(1) The eleventh upward special express train in the morning, due to the use of Pacific-type new locomotives, has increased speed and shortened travel time. Therefore, the departure time from Shanghai North Station is planned to change to 9:30 AM and arrive in Beijing at 4:24 PM.

(2) The nineteenth upward combined transport special express train in the afternoon will also use Pacific-type locomotives to shorten travel time. Therefore, the departure time can be delayed to 3:15 PM, allowing sufficient preparation after the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo combined transport train arrives at Shanghai North Station.

(3) The twenty-seventh upward overnight special express train, due to the use of Pacific-type new locomotives, plans to delay the departure time by 45 minutes, allowing passengers to board leisurely. The arrival time in Beijing will be 7:20 AM the next morning.

(4) The fourteenth downward special express train in the morning, because Xiaguan Station is far from the city center, passengers in the city often feel the current departure time is too early. Also, this train has combined transport connections. If combined transport passengers cannot catch it in time, they must wait for days. Therefore, it is planned to depart from Beijing at 10:00 AM.

(5) The twenty-fourth downward special express train in the afternoon plans to use Pacific-type locomotives to reduce travel time by 35 minutes.

(6) The twenty-eighth downward overnight special express train is still scheduled to depart from Beijing at 11:00 PM. Due to other train meeting schedules, it can only be advanced to arrive in Shanghai at 6:53 AM the next morning.

(B) Express Trains

(7) The seventh upward morning express train between Shanghai and Beijing is still scheduled to depart from Shanghai at 7:00 AM and arrive in Beijing at 3:50 PM.

(8) The departure time of the seventeenth upward afternoon express train is still appropriate, so there is no need to change it.

(9) The twelfth downward morning express train between Beijing and Shanghai is scheduled to depart from Beijing at 7:30 AM and arrive in Shanghai at 4:24 PM.

(10) The twenty-second downward afternoon express train between Beijing and Shanghai will delay the departure time by 25 minutes due to Jinpu combined transport connections.

(C) Slow Trains

(10)(1) The current thirteenth upward third and fourth class slow train between Beijing and Shanghai is delayed mainly because the dwell time at each station is too long. Each time it stops and the travel time between two stations is extremely tight. If the locomotive is damaged or the stations are crowded with passengers, it is easy to be delayed. Therefore, it often has to give way to the later afternoon express trains and special express trains, etc., so the delay upon arrival in Beijing is often three to four hours or more. Now it is planned to advance the departure of this train to 5:30 AM from Shanghai and arrive in Beijing at 2:53 PM. In the Shanghai-Wuxi section, it will only stop at the usual first and second class major stations. Above Wuxi, it will still stop at each station. In this way, the train can save stop time and avoid the delay of yielding to other trains midway. The passengers on this train mostly arrive at the station very early, so advancing the departure time is quite suitable for passenger needs, and long-distance passengers who arrive at the station early can also transfer to their destinations leisurely.

(10)(2) Currently, all problem trains in each district are equipped with first and second class seats to meet the needs of passengers. However, when passengers want to go to a station beyond the section of the train's route, or the express trains with first and second class seats do not stop at the station they want to go to, they often jointly write to request stops by express trains or special express trains, and so on. Therefore, it is planned to add a first, second, and third class Shanghai-Beijing slow train at 10:00 AM to remedy the above difficulties. Passengers traveling to and from small stations along the way who cannot catch the Shanghai-Beijing third and fourth class slow train or the third and fourth class trains do not stop at each station can take the first, second, and third class slow train. Generally, those who want to travel in first and second class can also avoid the regret of being unable to.

(10)(3) The reasons for the delay of the twentieth downward third and fourth class slow train between Beijing and Shanghai are the same as the thirteenth upward third and fourth class slow train mentioned above. Therefore, it is also planned to advance the departure to 8:00 AM from Beijing and stipulate that it yields to the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou combined transport special express train at Lingkou to avoid further unexpected delays. Long-distance third and fourth class passengers can also avoid arriving in Shanghai late at night. In the Wuxi-Shanghai North section, except for Suzhou, Kunshan, Anting, and Nanxiang stations, all other stations will not stop to save time and avoid delays.

However, for the convenience of passengers, it is planned to add a Shanghai-Wuxi third and fourth class local train, which arrives at Shanghai North Station 47 minutes earlier than the Beijing-Shanghai third and fourth class train. (20) The number of passengers on the current twelfth morning express train increases sharply in the Danyang-Changzhou section, so passengers west of Changzhou have no seats. To improve this situation, it is planned to use the Shanghai-Changzhou local train to run to Danyang the next day as a Changzhou-Danyang local train, and then run the train as a Dan-Shanghai local train before the Beijing-Shanghai morning express train to avoid congestion on the morning express train.

(21) The current Anting-Shanghai local train has few passengers at Anting and Huangdu stations, so it is planned to change it to a Shanghai-Shanghai local train to avoid low ridership. Because the distance between Shanghai North and Nanxiang is short, it is planned to transfer steam locomotives from the Shanghai-Shanghai line to save costs.

(22) The schedule of the Nanjing-Qianjiang local train is still suitable and no changes are planned.

(23) The downward Shanghai-Wuxi third and fourth class local train is for carrying passengers between Shanghai and Wuxi and to remedy the congestion of the Beijing-Shanghai third and fourth class train in the Shanghai-Wuxi section.

(24) The Dan-Shanghai local train is to avoid the congestion of the Beijing-Shanghai morning express train and to replace the canceled tenth Kunshan-Shanghai local train.

(25) There is no need to modify the schedule of the Changzhou-Shanghai and Shanghai-Wuxi South local trains.

(26) Most of the passengers on the current eighteenth Changzhou-Shanghai local train are absorbed by the sixteenth Shanghai-Wuxi local train, and the number of passengers in the Changzhou-Wuxi section not served by the sixteenth train is small. Therefore, the eighteenth train is almost redundant. It is planned to discontinue its operation to avoid low ridership. Implemented since yesterday. After the Shanghai-Shanghai Railway started running steam locomotives last year, there were 74 upward and downward trains every day, departing every 20 minutes. Passengers praised it for its convenience. Later, due to frequent locomotive breakdowns midway, there were many delays, and passengers complained. Recently, the railway bureau, in order to rectify the situation, re-stipulated the timetable for the upward and downward trains on the line. The original 74 Shanghai-Shanghai upward and downward trains have now been changed to 40, a reduction of 34. However, 40 local trains have been added from Shanghai Station to Jiangwan, which officially started yesterday. Because the number of trains between Shanghai and Shanghai has been reduced by almost half, the passengers on each upward and downward train were extremely crowded yesterday. There was no room to stand in the carriages, and passengers were dangerously hanging on the steps of the carriages. The situation was extremely dangerous. Although the railway bureau staff advised them, they did not pay attention, and passengers continued to arrive, all waiting for the next train because they could not board. Guo Jingluan Goes to Jinan

Investigate the Remains of Martyr Cai Gongshi 118

Request the Central Government to order the Shandong Provincial Government to assist in the investigation of the remains of martyr Cai Gongshi, who died in the May 3rd Massacre at the Jinan Diplomatic Office. It is unknown where the Japanese abandoned his remains. Because the Jinan Case has not been resolved, there is no way to investigate. After the Shandong Provincial Party Department exposed that the house owner Zhang Shuheng secretly rented the martyrdom site to the Japanese in an attempt to cover up the May 3rd Massacre, Mrs. Cai Gongshi, Guo Jingluan, repeatedly requested the Central Party Department, the National Government, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Shandong Provincial Government to investigate and find the remains separately. The details of the process have been recorded in previous reports. It was heard that Mrs. Cai originally planned to go to Jinan as soon as possible, but was unable to start due to illness. Recently, her condition has improved slightly. The Gongshi School, named in memory of martyr Cai, has also moved to new school buildings and started classes. Therefore, yesterday, she went to Nanjing to ask the Central Government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for instructions and set off for Jinan on the same day. The memorial to the National Government is recorded as follows: "Presenting the case of recovering from illness and going to Jinan to find the remains of martyr Cai Gongshi, humbly requesting the Shandong Provincial Government to grant assistance. I, Jingluan, lost my husband, martyr Cai Gongshi, in the May 3rd Massacre, and his remains in Jinan have not been found. The martyrdom site was rented to the Japanese by the house owner Zhang Shuheng. I requested the Shandong Provincial Government to confiscate the land and find the remains to appease the loyal soul. The case was handled by your government and the Executive Yuan, and the reply from the Shandong Provincial Government has been received recently, and I am notified by the Civil Affairs Office of your government. I am extremely grateful and moved. Although Jingluan has been unable to go to Jinan for a long time due to illness, she has secretly instructed Han Chunru, the father of Han Shuzhen, the secretary of the diplomatic office who died at the same time as martyr Cai, to go to investigate. The main points of his report are that the burial site of martyr Cai and others is roughly the same as that reported by the Jinan Public Security Bureau of Shandong Province, but in more detail. The martyrdom site is still piled with cotton, allowing mules and horses to enter and trample on it. According to his investigation, the martyrdom site did have the signboard of the Japanese Hua Kang Foreign Firm, and it was only changed to Da Zhong Hua Zhan after the Party Department exposed it. The Shandong Provincial Government's reply lists methods that focus on Jingluan and former comrades of martyr Cai who know the special features of martyr Cai's clothing and appearance to provide detailed descriptions before trying to find and bury them. Now, Jingluan's sick body has recovered slightly, and the tragic image of my deceased husband's martyrdom for the country breaks my heart. I have decided to personally go to Jinan to find the remains. Not only does my deceased husband have special markings on his teeth, but his decayed clothing can also be identified. (Omission) I urgently report to your government for review. However, Jingluan is an ordinary weak woman, and Jinan is a place where she has never set foot. I am very afraid that my knowledge and ability are weak and I cannot investigate. However, I think that my deceased husband died for the country in a diplomatic incident. I dare to humbly implore your government to grant permission to order the Shandong Provincial Government to instruct the Jinan Public Security Bureau to provide practical and effective assistance at any time and to seal off the martyrdom site so that the grave can be excavated to find the remains. As for the Shandong Provincial Party Committee and the Licheng County Party Department's proposal to rebuild the Martyr's Shrine at the site, the Shandong Provincial Government's reply to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs states that the shrine should be built to show the great integrity and encourage future generations. The special shrine for praising loyalty and martyrdom should be ordered by the National Government to facilitate preparations and show seriousness. I also ask your government to quickly approve the implementation. I will report to your government on the situation in Jinan at any time for your inspection and guidance. With tears in my eyes, I submit this petition, unable to restrain my impatience and awaiting orders. Respectfully presented to the Chairman of the National Government, Jiang Gongshi. Cai Guo Jingluan, Principal of Zhong School

French Aviators Did Not Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday 119

Whether they will travel today still depends on the weather. French aviators Maineux and Bellonte set off from Paris on the 2nd of this month in a Farman monoplane for a long-distance flight from Paris to Tokyo. They flew to Hong Kong the day before yesterday and were originally scheduled to fly directly to Shanghai from Hong Kong at 7:00 AM yesterday, expecting to arrive yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. However, the weather in the south has not improved, and the dense fog surrounding Hong Kong has not dissipated, so the two aviators decided to postpone their flight to Shanghai. However, the various sectors of the city did not know the truth and still went to Hongqiao Airport to welcome them. Later, the French Consul General notified the aircraft factory director Shen Dexie by telephone that the aviators had postponed their arrival in Shanghai, and they all returned disappointed. Whether the aviators will be able to arrive in Shanghai today still depends on the weather.

Street Vendors on Min'guo Road Resume Business 121

In the area of Min'guo Road in the French Concession, vegetable vendors have been setting up stalls for business. However, the stalls set up by the vendors did not comply with the police rules, so the French police strictly banned the stalls on the section of Xinqiao Street a few days ago in order to maintain traffic.
